 kisaan apni kul kamai se 46,000 rupee ke karj kii rakam lautaakar lagbhag 54,000 rupee kaa munafa prati hectare khet par kar letaa he
 As soon as the farmer is ready to harvest and sell after taking the loan from the cooperative bank, from farm to market, his challenge is to find the right customer for the crop
 aamtaur par kisaan ko sarkaar dwaara nirdhaarit samarthan mulya par apni fasal bechney kaa mauka mil jaataa he
 But the co-operative banks present here deduct Rs 46,000 of their loan from the farmer's one lakh rupees cell
 kisaan ke haath main fasal bechakar 54,000 rupee bachate hai
 So, let's say that the farmer has only half the money left to do farming by taking loans
 karj ke liye syrius nahin kisanasahakaari mandiyon main sahakaari bank kii nigaraanee main fasal bechney par kisaan ko sirf fasal kii kamai kaa aadha haath lagata he
 Hence, most farmers shy away from selling their crops at these cooperative mandis at the minimum support price
 aise main kisaan apni fasal ko oune-paune daam par (60 se 70 hajaar rupee) mandi main baithe bichauliyon ko dekar apana munafa nikaal lete hai
 As a result, farmers do not get the chance to increase their earnings per hectare by not taking the loan serially

 By doing this, the farmer gets more profit while he has to sell his crop at a lower rate from the cooperative mandis
 iske alaava mandi par fasal bechney ke liye kisaanon ko apni laagat par fasal ko mandi pahunchaana padataa he

 Cooperative banks usually make and issue a draft or check of the profit amount of the farmer
 lihaaja, fasal bechney ke 15-20 din ke baad unhen cash mil paata he
